\doxysubsubsection{Detailed Description}
Include \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{gtc_2type__aligned_8hpp}{glm/gtc/type\+\_\+aligned.\+hpp}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} to use the features of this extension.

Aligned types allowing SIMD optimizations of vectors and matrices types
